<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">There are no NaN n this dataset, datetimes are objects not datetime dtypes</h3><a id="user-content-there-are-no-nan-n-this-dataset-datetimes-are-objects-not-datetime-dtypes" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: There are no NaN n this dataset, datetimes are objects not datetime dtypes" href="#there-are-no-nan-n-this-dataset-datetimes-are-objects-not-datetime-dtypes"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-python notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="df['tpep_dropoff_datetime'] = pd.to_datetime(df['tpep_dropoff_datetime'])

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Creation of trip duration in minutes</h2><a id="user-content-creation-of-trip-duration-in-minutes" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Creation of trip duration in minutes" href="#creation-of-trip-duration-in-minutes"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-python notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="#create duration of ride field
df['ride_duration'] = df['tpep_dropoff_datetime'] - df['tpep_pickup_datetime']
df['ride_duration'] = df['ride_duration'].dt.total_seconds()/60"><pre><span class="pl-c">#create duration of ride field</span>
<span class="pl-s1">df</span>[<span class="pl-s">'ride_duration'</span>] <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">df</span>[<span class="pl-s">'tpep_dropoff_datetime'</span>] <span class="pl-c1">-</span> <span class="pl-s1">df</span>[<span class="pl-s">'tpep_pickup_datetime'</span>]
<span class="pl-s1">df</span>[<span class="pl-s">'ride_duration'</span>] <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">df</span>[<span class="pl-s">'ride_duration'</span>].<span class="pl-s1">dt</span>.<span class="pl-en">total_seconds</span>()<span class="pl-c1">/</span><span class="pl-c1">60</span></pre></div>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Analysis of trip_distance variable:  There are a number of outliers on he high end as well as 19 rows with a trip distance = 0.  These rows will be addressed in cleaning.</h3><a id="user-content-analysis-of-trip_distance-variable--there-are-a-number-of-outliers-on-he-high-end-as-well-as-19-rows-with-a-trip-distance--0--these-rows-will-be-addressed-in-cleaning" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Analysis of trip_distance variable:  There are a number of outliers on he high end as well as 19 rows with a trip distance = 0.  These rows will be addressed in cleaning." href="#analysis-of-trip_distance-variable--there-are-a-number-of-outliers-on-he-high-end-as-well-as-19-rows-with-a-trip-distance--0--these-rows-will-be-addressed-in-cleaning"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Ride Duration('ride_duration')</h2><a id="user-content-ride-durationride_duration" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Ride Duration('ride_duration')" href="#ride-durationride_duration"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Analysis:  There are again a number of outliers in this field as well as a number of zero values.  These will be addressed in cleaning.</h3><a id="user-content-analysis--there-are-again-a-number-of-outliers-in-this-field-as-well-as-a-number-of-zero-values--these-will-be-addressed-in-cleaning" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Analysis:  There are again a number of outliers in this field as well as a number of zero values.  These will be addressed in cleaning." href="#analysis--there-are-again-a-number-of-outliers-in-this-field-as-well-as-a-number-of-zero-values--these-will-be-addressed-in-cleaning"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Initial Analysis Passenger Counts('passenger_count')</h2><a id="user-content-initial-analysis-passenger-countspassenger_count" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Initial Analysis Passenger Counts('passenger_count')" href="#initial-analysis-passenger-countspassenger_count"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Most rides were single occupancy but a significant number were higher, the zero rider data will be addressed.</h3><a id="user-content-most-rides-were-single-occupancy-but-a-significant-number-were-higher-the-zero-rider-data-will-be-addressed" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Most rides were single occupancy but a significant number were higher, the zero rider data will be addressed." href="#most-rides-were-single-occupancy-but-a-significant-number-were-higher-the-zero-rider-data-will-be-addressed"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">General Analysis of data validity and cleanliness</h2><a id="user-content-general-analysis-of-data-validity-and-cleanliness" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: General Analysis of data validity and cleanliness" href="#general-analysis-of-data-validity-and-cleanliness"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>

    .dataframe tbody tr th:only-of-type {

#so the passenger count will have passenger count converted to 1(the median)
df_clean.loc[df_clean['passenger_count'] == 0, 'passenger_count'] = 1

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">We have elimionated 210 rows of data with problematic fields</h3><a id="user-content-we-have-elimionated-210-rows-of-data-with-problematic-fields" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: We have elimionated 210 rows of data with problematic fields" href="#we-have-elimionated-210-rows-of-data-with-problematic-fields"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Creating a new column that includes all of the required fares and tolls but eliminates the tip due to their discretionary nature.</h2><a id="user-content-creating-a-new-column-that-includes-all-of-the-required-fares-and-tolls-but-eliminates-the-tip-due-to-their-discretionary-nature" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Creating a new column that includes all of the required fares and tolls but eliminates the tip due to their discretionary nature." href="#creating-a-new-column-that-includes-all-of-the-required-fares-and-tolls-but-eliminates-the-tip-due-to-their-discretionary-nature"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-python notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="df_clean['total_fare_minus_tip']= df_clean['total_amount'] - df_clean['tip_amount']
"><pre><span class="pl-s1">df_clean</span>[<span class="pl-s">'total_fare_minus_tip'</span>]<span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">df_clean</span>[<span class="pl-s">'total_amount'</span>] <span class="pl-c1">-</span> <span class="pl-s1">df_clean</span>[<span class="pl-s">'tip_amount'</span>]</pre></div>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-python notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="#Determining likely errors in fares by creating a new column dollars per mile
df_clean['dollars_per_mile'] = df_clean['total_fare_minus_tip']/df_clean['trip_distance']
df_clean.head(3)"><pre><span class="pl-c">#Determining likely errors in fares by creating a new column dollars per mile</span>
<span class="pl-s1">df_clean</span>[<span class="pl-s">'dollars_per_mile'</span>] <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">df_clean</span>[<span class="pl-s">'total_fare_minus_tip'</span>]<span class="pl-c1">/</span><span class="pl-s1">df_clean</span>[<span class="pl-s">'trip_distance'</span>]
<span class="pl-s1">df_clean</span>.<span class="pl-en">head</span>(<span class="pl-c1">3</span>)</pre></div>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">An excessively large number of rows meet the statistical definition of outliers (935). <div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">The top 5 dollars per mile rides are the most extreme and will be deleted.</h3><a id="user-content-the-top-5-dollars-per-mile-rides-are-the-most-extreme-and-will-be-deleted" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: The top 5 dollars per mile rides are the most extreme and will be deleted." href="#the-top-5-dollars-per-mile-rides-are-the-most-extreme-and-will-be-deleted"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
